posted:Posted April 3, 2024
msg:From food to accommodation, I basically felt that the overall experience was smooth from the beginning to the end. I would only post some pictures for recommendation if I really have something to share. It was the first time that I was asked by the merchant, and then it was to change a delayed check-out to 14:00, which was a little bit of a slippery experience.
There was a big spider in the room, and the room lady was very good. She caught it directly with a towel and solved the trouble in time.
The front desk was very good. It was not yet 14:00 when we checked out. The front desk recommended that we could try taking photos in Hanfu, giving us plenty of time to experience it.
It was my mother's birthday, so I took her to a quiet and comfortable place to stay and relax. Maybe because it was the off-season, we chatted and drank tea in the courtyard room and the river view room at night. There was no one living in the surrounding rooms, so we didn't worry about the noise. We said it was very relaxing and healing, and the elderly were happy.
I was used to delaying check-out with Ctrip benefits before, so I didn't see the hotel's rejection message when I exchanged it this time. I didn't know that I had to check out until 12:00 noon, so there was a little episode that was not smooth. But I was very satisfied with the environment, room facilities and geographical location. The breakfast mainly consists of Leshan specialty snacks. Compared with the breakfast of hotels of the same type and price, the variety is still a little less, but the environment experience is very good.
It is OK to stay here with children and family.

name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Courtyard Deluxe Family Friendly Room - Near River (2 Beds)
info:Stayed in August 2021
info:Family
info:13 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted August 15, 2021
msg:A hotel in the Leshan Giant Buddha Scenic Area, if you want to go to the Leshan Giant Buddha, it is very convenient to live here.
Let me talk about the advantages:
1. The room facilities are very new. There are three sinks in the parent-child room. There is a small round table to facilitate office work. It would be better if the tea table can be replaced by a small tent for children.
2. The hotel is very quiet, with the riverfront behind it, it is very comfortable to take a walk
3. On Lingyun Road, walk 1.4 kilometers to reach the north gate of Leshan Giant Buddha, buy a ticket online and swipe your ID card to enter the scenic spot
4. There are not too many types of breakfast, but the quality and taste are not bad
Areas to be improved:
1. The swimming pool is not open. The hotelâ€™s explanation is due to the weather, but the other hotel swimming pools on the left and right sides are all open that day.
2. The soft facilities in the room need to be paid, and the TV program is 8 yuan for 12 hours. If the hotel gives it away, I think the experience will be different. The snacks and drinks are also charged. Compared with the free drinks, good night snacks and mung bean soup in the previous Ya'an hotel , There is still a gap in my heart
3. The hotel does not have a parking lot. It needs to be parked in the Leshan Giant Buddha North parking lot. The cost is 45 per night, and the hotel guests need to take care of themselves. The experience is not very good.
4. Except for hotel restaurants, there are not many places to eat around, so you need to drive to the city to eat
In short, if you go to Leshan Giant Buddha, I still recommend Sanjiangyue Hotel, but please be sure to highlight the "vacation" features, swimming pools, children's facilities, etc., not just a place to sleep for one night.
